class=\"careers-left span_1_of_3\">\n\t\t<section class=\"primary-sidebar careers-sidebar float-column full-width no-min\">\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t<div class=\"menu-3-careers-menu-container\"><ul .careers-left -->\n\t\n\t\n\t\n\t<!-- MAIN CONTENT -->\n\t<div class=\"careers-right span_2_of_3\">\t\n\t\t<section class=\"single-blog-wrapper float-column full-width two-column-content\">\n\t\t\t<h1 class=\"blogpost-title\">\n\t\t\t\tGraphic Design Intern (Spring), Los Angeles\t\t\t</h1>\n\t\t\t<div class=\"blog-content\">\n\t\t\t\t<h4>Position Overview and Responsibilities</h4>\n\n<p>FleishmanHillard Los Angeles has an immediate opening for a graphic design intern to work with some of the very best public relations professionals in the industry on a variety of accounts across consumer, technology and lifestyle.</p>\n\n<p>We are looking for an individual who is passionate about visual communications, graphic design, is eager to learn, and is as committed to doing great work as we are. Interns should have the ability to juggle a wide variety of projects and work with varying production styles with demanding client expectations and deadlines. Go-getters with a positive attitudes and the drive to learn and contribute to the team thrive best in this role.</p>\n\n<p>Candidates should possess advanced design skills and well-rounded design experience as demonstrated through a robust portfolio and “real world” work. The FleishmanHillard experience provides the opportunity to grow personally and professionally through exposure to client service and the inner workings of an international communications firm.</p>\n\n<p>This is a full-time, paid internship with a three-month term. We are only considering candidates based in the Southern California area.</p>\n\n<p>Responsibilities Include:</p>\n\n<p>Working with the creative team to develop and produce:</p>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li>Social media content including Facebook and other social/online visuals, infographics, and promotional elements</li>\n\t<li>Logos/key visuals and style guides</li>\n\t<li>PowerPoint templates, presentation boards, and hardcopy proposals</li>\n\t<li>Working with diverse personalities across the firm, managing a busy workflow consisting of multiple projects with tight deadlines</li>\n\t<li>Participating in creative brainstorms</li>\n\t<li>Other duties as assigned</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h4>Qualifications</h4>\n\n<p>Candidates are expected to have high-level skills in the following areas:</p>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li>PowerPoint design</li>\n\t<li>Creative strategy</li>\n\t<li>Logo development and design</li>\n\t<li>Photo editing and manipulation</li>\n\t<li>Print/print process experience</li>\n\t<li>Branding concept and design</li>\n\t<li>Product styling and photography</li>\n\t<li>Social media design</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>The following additional skills are a plus:</p>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li>Packaging design</li>\n\t<li>Mobile app design</li>\n\t<li>UI/UX design</li>\n\t<li>Web design</li>\n\t<li>Illustration</li>\n\t<li>Multi-Media (i.e. print, outdoor, guerilla, etc.)</li>\n\t<li>Trade Show Material design</li>\n\t<li>Required Software Proficiency</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>Candidates are expected to have expert skills with the following software programs on the Macintosh platform:</p>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li>Illustrator</li>\n\t<li>Photoshop</li>\n\t<li>InDesign</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>Candidates should also be proficient in the following software programs:</p>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li>Lightroom</li>\n\t<li>Dreamweaver</li>\n\t<li>Premier and/or After Effects</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>&nbsp;Applications are welcomed from graduates with concentrations in all major communications areas, but backgrounds in communications design, graphic design, mass media, digital media, and public relations are given first consideration.</p>\n\n<p>If this description is an accurate representation of your arsenal of skills, please send us the following:</p>\n\n<ul>\n\t<li>Either a link to your website or video channel showcasing your portfolio</li>\n\t<li>A cover letter</li>\n\t<li>Your resume</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>Please do not contact the office directly to apply – only resumes submitted through this website will be considered.</p>\n\n<p>FleishmanHillard Los Angeles will consider qualified candidates with criminal histories in a manner consistent with the Los Angeles Fair Chance Initiative for Hiring Ordinance.</p>\n\n<h4>About FleishmanHillard</h4>\n\n<p>FleishmanHillard specializes in public relations, reputation management, public affairs, brand marketing, digital strategy, social engagement and content strategy. FleishmanHillard was named PRWeek’s 2014 Global Agency of the Year, “Standout Agency” on Advertising Age’s 2013 A-List; NAFE’s “Top 50 Companies for Executive Women” for 2010-2016; and among PRWeek’s 2013 “Best Places to Work.” The firm’s award-winning work is widely heralded, including at the Cannes International Festival of Creativity. FleishmanHillard is part of Omnicom Public Relations Group, a division of Omnicom Group Inc., and has more than 85 offices in 30 countries, plus affiliates in 43 countries. Visit us at <a href=\"http://www.fleishmanhillard.com\">www.fleishmanhillard.com</a>.</p>\n\n<h4>About Omnicom Public Relations Group</h4>\n\n<p><a href=\"http://www.omnicomprgroup.com/\">Omnicom Public Relations Group</a> is a global collective of three of the top global public relations agencies worldwide and eight specialist agencies in public affairs, marketing to women, fashion, global health strategy and corporate social responsibility. It encompasses more than 6,000 public relations professionals in more than 330 offices worldwide who provide their expertise to companies, government agencies, NGOs and nonprofits across a wide range of industries. Omnicom Public Relations Group delivers for clients through a relentless focus on talent, continuous pursuit of innovation and a culture steeped in collaboration. Omnicom Public Relations Group is part of the DAS Group of Companies, a division of Omnicom Group Inc. that includes more than 200 companies in a wide range of marketing disciplines including advertising, public relations, healthcare, customer relationship management, events, promotional marketing, branding and research.</p>\n\n<p>FleishmanHillard is committed to equal employment opportunity and affirmative action. FleishmanHillard does not discriminate in any aspect of employment on the basis of race, color, religion, national origin, ancestry, gender, sexual orientation, gender identity and/or expression, age, veteran status, disability, or any other characteristic protected by federal, state, or local employment discrimination laws where FleishmanHillard does business. Our policy is to employ, advance, and reasonably accommodate all qualified employees and applicants.</p>\n\n<p>If you need assistance reviewing career opportunities or completing an application,
